3778 // BAND 5: High-Shelf filter
3779 else if(Display.currentBand == 5) {
3780 EQ_BAND5.cutoff = Display.Filter_Cutoff[Display.currentBand-1];
3781 SetupHighShelf(&EQ_BAND5, EQ_BAND5.cutoff, EQ_BAND5.Q, EQ_BAND5.dBGain);
3782 }
3783 break;
3784 case 3:
3785 // Gain
3786
3787 /*****************************
3788 * @brief HS / LS / PEQ Gain: -18dB to 6dB
3789 * @brief Scaling 4095 (ADC_value) to a range of 24dB by dividing with 170.625
3790 * @brief Center around 0dB by subtracting (4095/(2*170.625))
3791 * @brief Subtract 6dB for final adjust
3792 ******************************/
3793 Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1] = ((float)Display.ADC2inputs[2] / 170.625)-(4095/(2*170.625))-6;
3794
3795 // BAND 1: Low-Shelf filter
3796 if(Display.currentBand == 1) {
3797 EQ_BAND1.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3798 SetupLowShelf(&EQ_BAND1, EQ_BAND1.cutoff, EQ_BAND1.Q, EQ_BAND1.dBGain);
3799 }
3800 // BAND 2: Peaking-EQ
3801 else if(Display.currentBand == 2) {
3802 EQ_BAND2.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3803 SetupPeakingEQ(&EQ_BAND2, EQ_BAND2.cutoff, EQ_BAND2.Q, EQ_BAND2.dBGain);
3804 }
3805 // BAND 3: Peaking-EQ
3806 else if(Display.currentBand == 3) {
3807 EQ_BAND3.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3808 SetupPeakingEQ(&EQ_BAND3, EQ_BAND3.cutoff, EQ_BAND3.Q, EQ_BAND3.dBGain);
3809 }
3810 // BAND 4: Peaking-EQ
3811 else if(Display.currentBand == 4) {
3812 EQ_BAND4.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3813 SetupPeakingEQ(&EQ_BAND4, EQ_BAND4.cutoff, EQ_BAND4.Q, EQ_BAND4.dBGain);
3814 }
3815 // BAND 5: High-Shelf filter
3816 else if(Display.currentBand == 5) {
3817 EQ_BAND5.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3818 SetupHighShelf(&EQ_BAND5, EQ_BAND5.cutoff, EQ_BAND5.Q, EQ_BAND5.dBGain);
3819 }
3820 break;
3821 case 4:
3822 // Q-Factor Source
3823 break;
3824 case 5:
3825 // Cutoff Source
3826 break;
3827 case 6:
3828 // Gain Source
3829 break;
3830 default:
3831 break;
3832 }
3833 }
